                    [32m'> Store `codeVerifier` securely on-device between generating the auth URL and handling the callback. For mobile apps, use platform secure storage (iOS Keychain, Android Keystore). For CLI apps, consider OS credential storage. The verifier must survive app restarts during the auth flow.\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'See the [AuthKit documentation](https://workos.com/docs/authkit) for details on PKCE authentication.\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'### PKCE with Confidential Clients\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Server-side apps can also use PKCE alongside the client secret for defense in depth (recommended by OAuth 2.1):\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```ts\n'[39m +
                    [32m"const workos = new WorkOS('sk_...'); // With API key\n"[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'// Use PKCE even with API key for additional security\n'[39m +
                    [32m'const { url, codeVerifier } =\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  await workos.userManagement.getAuthorizationUrlWithPKCE({\n'[39m +
                    [32m"    provider: 'authkit',\n"[39m +
                    [32m"    redirectUri: 'https://example.com/callback',\n"[39m +
                    [32m"    clientId: 'client_...',\n"[39m +
                    [32m'  });\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'// Both client_secret AND code_verifier will be sent\n'[39m +
                    [32m'const { accessToken } = await workos.userManagement.authenticateWithCode({\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  code: authorizationCode,\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  codeVerifier,\n'[39m +
                    [32m"  clientId: 'client_...',\n"[39m +
                    [32m'});\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\n'[39m +
